= pd.concat([pd.read_csv(base/f'message_metadata_{i:03d}.csv') for i in range(1,7)], ignore_index=True)\ndeps = pd.read_csv(base/'task_dependency_001.csv')\n\n# Business minutes within 09:00-17:00 every day\nWORK_START=9*60\nWORK_END=17*60\nDAY=24*60\nWORKDAY=8*60\n\ndef bh_minutes(start, end):\n    if pd.isna(start) or pd.isna(end):\n        return np.nan\n    if not isinstance(start, pd.Timestamp):\n        start = pd.Timestamp(start)\n    if not isinstance(end, pd.Timestamp):\n        end = pd.Timestamp(end)\n    if end <= start:\n        return 0.0\n    sday = start.normalize()\n    eday = end.normalize()\n    def overlap_day(day, a, b):\n        ws = day + pd.Timedelta(minutes=WORK_START)\n        we = day + pd.Timedelta(minutes=WORK_END)\n        ss = max(a, ws)\n        ee = min(b, we)\n        return max(0.0, (ee-ss).total_seconds()/60.0)\n    if sday == eday:\n        return overlap_day(sday, start, end)\n    total = overlap_day(sday, start, sday + pd.Timedelta(days=1))\n    total += overlap_day(eday, eday, end)\n    days_between = (eday - sday).days - 1\n    if days_between > 0:\n        total += days_between * WORKDAY\n    return msgs['minute_of_day'].between(WORK_START, WORK_END-1)\n\n# Task metadata on assignments\nassign = assign.merge(tasks[['task_id','task_type','priority','complexity_score','risk_score','created_at','completed_at']], on='task_id', how='left')\nassign['duration_bh_min'] = [bh_minutes(s,e) for s,e in zip(approvals['requested_at'], approvals['resolved_at'])]\n\n# Deduplicate QA/deploy via assignments for duration metrics? use assignment duration by role for tester/deployer.\n\n# Helper to compute excess vs peer baseline within context\nfrom math import log1p\n\ndef add_excess(df, worker_col, dur_col, context_cols, min_group=20):\n    g = df.groupby(context_cols)[dur_col]\n    med = g.transform('median')\n    cnt = g.transform('size')\n    global_med = df[dur_col].median()\n    baseline = med.where(cnt>=min_group, global_med)\n    df = df.copy()\n    df['baseline'] = baseline\n    df['excess_min'] = (df[dur_col] - baseline).clip(lower=0)\n    df['ratio'] = df[dur_col] / baseline.replace(0,np.nan)\n    return df\n\n# Focus implementation-like assignment roles (exclude reviewer/approver/tester/deployer because separate tables exist)\nimpl_roles = ['owner','implement','triage','design','architecture_reviewer','verify','investigate','decompose','security_reviewer']\nassign_perf = assign[assign['assignment_role'].isin(impl_roles)].copy()\nassign_perf = add_excess(assign_perf, 'employee_id', 'duration_bh_min', ['assignment_role','task_type'])\nreviews_perf = add_excess(reviews, 'reviewer_id', 'duration_bh_min', ['task_type','review_outcome'])\napprovals_perf = add_excess(approvals, 'approver_id', 'duration_bh_min', ['approval_type'])\n\n# Aggregate stage-specific performance\nperf_parts = []\nfor label, df, worker_col in [\n    ('assign', assign_perf, 'employee_id'),\n    ('review', reviews_perf, 'reviewer_id'),\n    ('approval', approvals_perf, 'approver_id'),\n]:\n    agg = df.groupby(worker_col).agg(\n        n=(dur_col:='duration_bh_min','size'),\n        mean_min=(dur_col,'mean'),\n        median_min=(dur_col,'median'),\n        excess_min=('excess_min','sum'),\n        mean_ratio=('ratio','mean')\n    )\n    agg.columns = [f'{label}_{c}' for c in agg.columns]\n    agg.index.name='employee_id'\n    perf_parts.append(agg)\nperf = pd.concat(perf_parts, axis=1).fillna(0)\n\n# More detailed per-role assignment performance\nassign_role_agg = assign_perf.groupby(['employee_id','assignment_role']).agg(n=('duration_bh_min','size'), med=('duration_bh_min','median'), excess=('excess_min','sum')).reset_index()\n\n# Load metrics: counts and msgs[msgs['in_hours']].groupby('sender_id').size().rename('messages_sent_in_hours')\nmsg_recv = msgs[msgs['in_hours']].groupby('receiver_id').size().rename('messages_recv_in_hours')\nmeet_hours = meet_part.groupby('employee_id')['meeting_minutes_bh'].sum().div(60).rename('meeting_hours')\nmeet_count = meet_part.groupby('employee_id').size().rename('meetings')\norganizer_count = meet.groupby('organizer_id').size().rename('organized_meetings')\n\n# Request load: review/approval counts; assignment counts\nload = pd.concat([\n    assign.groupby('employee_id').size().rename('assignments'),\n    reviews.groupby('reviewer_id').size().rename('reviews'),\n    approvals.groupby('approver_id').size().rename('approvals'),\n    msg_sent, msg_recv, meet_hours, meet_count, organizer_count,\n], axis=1).fillna(0)\nload.index.name='employee_id'\n\n# Concurrent load approximation for assignments/reviews/approvals: max active open items sampled at event endpoints\nintervals = []\nfor df, worker_col, s_col, e_col, kind in [\n    (assign, 'employee_id', 'assigned_at', 'unassigned_at', 'assignment'),\n    (reviews, 'reviewer_id', 'requested_at', 'completed_at', 'review'),\n    (approvals, 'approver_id', 'requested_at', 'resolved_at', 'approval'),\n]:\n    sub = df[[worker_col,s_col,e_col]].dropna().copy()\n    sub.columns=['employee_id','start','end']\n    sub['kind']=kind\n    intervals.append(sub)\nintervals = pd.concat(intervals, ignore_index=True)\n# sweep line per employee\nconcurrency = {}\nfor emp_id, sub in intervals.groupby('employee_id'):\n    events=[]\n    for s,e in zip(sub['start'], sub['end']):\n        events.append((s,1))\n        events.append((e,-1))\n    events.sort(key=lambda x:(x[0], x[1]))\n    cur=maxc=0\n    for _,delta in events:\n        cur += delta\n        if cur>maxc: maxc=cur\n    concurrency[emp_id]=maxc\nconcurrency = pd.Series(concurrency, name='max_concurrency')\n\n# Impact via dependencies: assign blocking-task excess to employees on blocking tasks\n# Compute task completion excess vs similar tasks (task_type + complexity bucket + priority)\ntasks['duration_bh_min'] = [bh_minutes(s,e) for s,e in zip(tasks['created_at'], tasks['completed_at'])]\ntasks['complexity_bin'] = pd.cut(tasks['complexity_score'], bins=[0,3,5,7,10], labels=['1-3','4-5','6-7','8-10'], include_lowest=True)\ntask_med = tasks.groupby(['task_type','complexity_bin','priority'])['duration_bh_min'].transform('median')\ntask_cnt = tasks.groupby(['task_type','complexity_bin','priority'])['duration_bh_min'].transform('size')\nglobal_med = tasks['duration_bh_min'].median()\ntasks['baseline'] = task_med.where(task_cnt>=15, global_med)\ntasks['excess_min'] = (tasks['duration_bh_min']-tasks['baseline']).clip(lower=0)\n\n# number/weight of dependents per task\nblocked_counts = deps.groupby('blocking_task_id').size().rename('blocked_task_count')\n# blocked wait duration weighted to blocking task\nwait = deps.copy()\nwait['wait_bh_min'] = [bh_minutes(s,e) for s,e in zip(wait['created_at'], wait['resolved_at'])]\nblocked_wait = wait.groupby('blocking_task_id')['wait_bh_min'].sum().rename('blocked_wait_bh_min')\n\ntask_impact = tasks[['task_id','excess_min']].merge(blocked_counts, left_on='task_id', right_index=True, how='left').merge(blocked_wait, left_on='task_id', right_index=True, how='left')\ntask_impact[['blocked_task_count','blocked_wait_bh_min']] = task_impact[['blocked_task_count','blocked_wait_bh_min']].fillna(0)\n# attribute task impact to owner/implement assignees on task\nresponsible = assign[assign['assignment_role'].isin(['owner','implement'])][['task_id','employee_id','assignment_role']].drop_duplicates()\nresp_imp = responsible.merge(task_impact, on='task_id', how='left')\n# share equally among responsible employees per task\nshare = resp_imp.groupby('task_id').size().rename('nresp')\nresp_imp = resp_imp.merge(share, on='task_id', how='left')\nresp_imp['task_excess_share'] = resp_imp['excess_min']/resp_imp['nresp']\nresp_imp['blocked_wait_share'] = resp_imp['blocked_wait_bh_min']/resp_imp['nresp']\nimpact = resp_imp.groupby('employee_id').agg(\n    impacted_task_excess=('task_excess_share','sum'),\n    blocked_wait_bh_min=('blocked_wait_share','sum'),\n    blocking_tasks=('task_id','nunique')\n)\n\n# Join everything\nsummary = emp[['employee_id','role','seniority_level','department']].merge(perf, on='employee_id', how='left').merge(load, on='employee_id', how='left').merge(concurrency, on='employee_id', how='left').merge(impact, on='employee_id', how='left')\nsummary = summary.fillna(0)\n\n# Standardized scores within seniority to avoid blaming managers for review load alone\n# Compute workload z-like ranks\nfor c in ['assignments','reviews','approvals','messages_sent_in_hours','messages_recv_in_hours','meeting_hours','meetings','organized_meetings','max_concurrency']:\n    summary[c+'_pct'] = summary.groupby('seniority_level')[c].rank(pct=True)\n\nfor c in ['assign_excess_min','review_excess_min','approval_excess_min','impacted_task_excess','blocked_wait_bh_min']:\n    summary[c+'_pct'] = summary.groupby('seniority_level')[c].rank(pct=True)\n\n# Combined scores\nsummary['delay_score'] = (\n    0.35*summary['assign_excess_min_pct'] +\n    0.30*summary['review_excess_min_pct'] +\n    0.20*summary['approval_excess_min_pct'] +\n    0.10*summary['impacted_task_excess_pct'] +\n    0.05*summary['blocked_wait_bh_min_pct']\n)\nsummary['load_score'] = (\n    0.20*summary['assignments_pct'] +\n    0.20*summary['reviews_pct'] +\n    0.15*summary['approvals_pct'] +\n    0.15*summary['meeting_hours_pct'] +\n    0.10*summary['messages_sent_in_hours_pct'] +\n    0.10*summary['messages_recv_in_hours_pct'] +\n    0.10*summary['max_concurrency_pct']\n)\nsummary['bottleneck_score'] = 0.65*summary['delay_score'] + 0.35*summary['load_score']\n\n# only employees with some meaningful activity and delay\nsummary['activity'] = summary[['assignments','reviews','approvals']].sum(axis=1)\nres = summary.sort_values(['bottleneck_score','delay_score','activity'], ascending=False)\ncols = ['employee_id','role','seniority_level','department','bottleneck_score','delay_score','load_score','activity',\n        'assign_excess_min','review_excess_min','approval_excess_min','impacted_task_excess','blocked_wait_bh_min',\n        'assignments','reviews','approvals','meeting_hours','meetings','messages_sent_in_hours','messages_recv_in_hours','max_concurrency']\nprint(res[cols].head(40).to_string(index=False))\nprint('\\\\nTop assignment-role outliers:')\nfor eid in res['employee_id'].head(15):\n    sub = assign_role_agg[assign_role_agg['employee_id']==eid].sort_values('excess', ascending=False).head(5)\n    if not sub.empty:\n        print('\\\\nEmployee', eid)\n        print(sub.to_string(index=False))\nPY\"","aggregated_output":"","exit_code":null,"status":"in_progress"}}

reviews.merge(tasks[['task_id','task_type','priority','complexity_score','risk_score']], on='task_id', how='left')\nreviews['duration_bh_min'] = [bh_minutes(s,e) for s,e in zip(reviews['requested_at'], reviews['completed_at'])]\napprovals = approvals.merge(tasks[['task_id','task_type','priority','complexity_score','risk_score']], on='task_id', how='left')\napprovals['duration_bh_min'] = [bh_minutes(s,e) for s,e in zip(approvals['requested_at'], approvals['resolved_at'])]\n\n# meetings/messages\nmeet['meeting_hours'] = (meet['end_time'] - meet['start_time']).dt.total_seconds()/3600\nmeet_part = mp.merge(meet[['meeting_id','meeting_hours','meeting_type','start_time']], on='meeting_id', how='left')\nmsgs['minute'] = msgs['timestamp'].dt.hour*60 + msgs['timestamp'].dt.minute\nmsgs['in_hours'] = msgs['minute'].between(WORK_START, WORK_END-1)\n\n# task durations / dependency impact\ntasks['duration_bh_min'] = [bh_minutes(s,e) for s,e in zip(tasks['created_at'], tasks['completed_at'])]\ntasks['complexity_bin'] = pd.cut(tasks['complexity_score'], bins=[0,3,5,7,10], labels=['1-3','4-5','6-7','8-10'], include_lowest=True)\n\n\ndef add_baseline(df, dur_col, group_cols, min_group=15):\n    df = df.copy()\n    med = df.groupby(group_cols)[dur_col].transform('median')\n    size = df.groupby(group_cols)[dur_col].transform('size')\n    global_med = df[dur_col].median()\n    df['baseline'] = med.where(size >= min_group, global_med)\n    df['excess_min'] = (df[dur_col] - df['baseline']).clip(lower=0)\n    df['ratio'] = df[dur_col] / df['baseline'].replace(0,np.nan)\n    return df\n\nimpl_roles = ['owner','implement','triage','design','architecture_reviewer','verify','investigate','decompose','security_reviewer']\nassign_perf = add_baseline(assign[assign['assignment_role'].isin(impl_roles)], 'duration_bh_min', ['assignment_role','task_type'])\nreviews_perf = add_baseline(reviews, 'duration_bh_min', ['task_type','review_outcome'])\napprovals_perf = add_baseline(approvals, 'duration_bh_min', ['approval_type'])\ntasks_perf = add_baseline(tasks, 'duration_bh_min', ['task_type','complexity_bin','priority'])\n\ndeps['wait_bh_min'] = [bh_minutes(s,e) for s,e in responsible.groupby('task_id').size().rename('nresp').reset_index()\nresponsible = responsible.merge(resp_counts, on='task_id', how='left')\nresponsible['task_excess_share'] = responsible['excess_min']/responsible['nresp']\nresponsible['blocked_wait_share'] = responsible['blocked_wait_bh_min']/responsible['nresp']\nimpact = responsible.groupby('employee_id').agg(\n    impacted_task_excess=('task_excess_share','sum'),\n    blocked_wait_bh_min=('blocked_wait_share','sum'),\n    blocking_tasks=('task_id','nunique')\n).reset_index()\n\n# performance 'approver_id'),\n]:\n    agg = df.groupby(worker_col).agg(\n        n=('duration_bh_min','size'),\n        mean_min=('duration_bh_min','mean'),\n        median_min=('duration_bh_min','median'),\n        excess_min=('excess_min','sum'),\n        mean_ratio=('ratio','mean')\n    ).reset_index().rename(columns={worker_col:'employee_id'})\n    agg = agg.rename(columns={c:f'{label}_{c}' for c in summary.merge(approvals.groupby('approver_id').size().rename('approvals').reset_index().rename(columns={'approver_id':'employee_id'}), on='employee_id', how='left')\nsummary = = summary.merge(meet_part.groupby('employee_id')['meeting_hours'].sum().reset_index(), on='employee_id', how='left')\nsummary = summary.merge(impact, on='employee_id', how='left')\nsummary = summary.fillna(0)\n\n# concurrency\nintervals = []\nfor df, worker_col, s_col, e_col in [\n    (assign, 'employee_id', 'assigned_at', 'unassigned_at'),\n    (reviews, 'reviewer_id', 'requested_at', 'completed_at'),\n    (approvals, 'approver_id', 'requested_at', 'resolved_at'),\n]:\n    sub = df[[worker_col,s_col,e_col]].dropna().copy()\n    sub.columns=['employee_id','start','end']\n    intervals.append(sub)\nintervals = pd.concat(intervals, ignore_index=True)\nconc = []\nfor eid, sub in intervals.groupby('employee_id'):\n    events=[]\n    for s,e in zip(sub['start'], sub['end']):\n        events.append((s,1))\n        events.append((e,-1))\n    events.sort(key=lambda x:(x[0], x[1]))\n    cur=0; maxc=0\n    for _,delta in events:\n        cur += delta\n        if cur > maxc: maxc = cur\n    conc.append((eid,maxc))\nconc = pd.DataFrame(conc, eday=e.normalize()\n    def ov(day,a,b):\n        ws=day+pd.Timedelta(hours=9); we=day+pd.Timedelta(hours=17)\n        ss=max(a,ws); ee=min(b,we)\n        return max(0.0,(ee-ss).total_seconds()/60)\n    if sday==eday: return ov(sday,s,e)\n    return ov(sday,s,sday+pd.Timedelta(days=1))+ov(eday,eday,e)+max(0,(eday-sday).days-1)*480\nappr['dur']=[bh(s,e) for s,e in zip(appr.requested_at,appr.resolved_at)]\nmed=appr.groupby('approval_type')['dur'].transform('median'); cnt=df.groupby(group)['dur'].transform('size'); b=med.where(cnt>=10, df.dur.median())\n    out=df.copy(); out['excess']=(out.dur-b).clip(lower=0); out['ratio']=out.dur/b.replace(0,np.nan); return out\n\na=add_base(assign[assign.assignment_role.isin(['owner','implement','triage','design','architecture_reviewer','verify','investigate','decompose','security_reviewer'])],['assignment_role','task_type'])\nr=add_base(reviews,['task_type','review_outcome'])\np=add_base(appr,['approval_type'])\nt=add_base(tasks,['task_type','complexity_bin','priority'])\nblock=deps.groupby('blocking_task_id')['wait'].sum().reset_index().rename(columns={'blocking_task_id':'task_id','wait':'blocked_wait'})\nresp=assign[assign.assignment_role.isin(['owner','implement'])][['task_id','employee_id']].drop_duplicates().merge(t[['task_id','excess']],on='task_id',how='left').merge(block,on='task_id',how='left').fillna({'blocked_wait':0})\nresp['nresp']=resp.groupby('task_id')['employee_id'].transform('count'); resp['task_excess']=resp['excess']/resp['nresp']; resp['blocked_wait_share']=resp['blocked_wait']/resp['nresp']\nmeet['hrs']=(meet.end_time-meet.start_time).dt.total_seconds()/3600; mhrs=mp.merge(meet[['meeting_id','hrs']],on='meeting_id').groupby('employee_id')['hrs'].sum().rename('meeting_hours').reset_index()\nmsgs['in_hours']=(msgs.timestamp.dt.hour*60+msgs.timestamp.dt.minute).between(540,1019)\nsent=msgs[msgs.in_hours].groupby('sender_id').size().rename('sent').reset_index().rename(columns={'sender_id':'employee_id'})\nrecv=msgs[msgs.in_hours].groupby('receiver_id').size().rename('recv').reset_index().rename(columns={'receiver_id':'employee_id'})\n\nm=emp[['employee_id','role','seniority_level']].copy()\nfor lab,df,col,val in [\n    ('assign_excess',a,'employee_id','excess'),('assign_ratio',a,'employee_id','ratio'),\n    ('review_excess',r,'reviewer_id','excess'),('review_ratio',r,'reviewer_id','ratio'),\n    ('approval_excess',p,'approver_id','excess'),('approval_ratio',p,'approver_id','ratio'),\n]:\n    g=getattr(df.groupby(col)[val],'sum' if 'excess' in lab else 'mean')().reset_index().rename(columns={col:'employee_id',val:lab})\n    m=m.merge(g,on='employee_id',how='left')\nfor lab,df,col in [('assignments',assign,'employee_id'),('reviews',reviews,'reviewer_id'),('approvals',appr,'approver_id')]:\n    g=df.groupby(col).size().rename(lab).reset_index().rename(columns={col:'employee_id'}); m=m.merge(g,on='employee_id',how='left')\nm=m.merge(resp.groupby('employee_id')['task_excess'].sum().reset_index(),on='employee_id',how='left')\nm=m.merge(resp.groupby('employee_id')['blocked_wait_share'].sum().reset_index(),on='employee_id',how='left')\nm=m.merge(mhrs,on='employee_id',how='left').merge(sent,on='employee_id',how='left').merge(recv,on='employee_id',how='left').fillna(0)\n# add percentiles within seniority as normalized features\nfeats=['assign_excess','assign_ratio','review_excess','review_ratio','approval_excess','approval_ratio','assignments','reviews','approvals','task_excess','blocked_wait_share','meeting_hours','sent','recv']\nfor c in feats:\n    m[c+'_pct']=m.groupby('seniority_level')[c].rank(pct=True)\nX=m[[c+'_pct' for c in feats]].values\nclf=IsolationForest(random_state=0, contamination=0.06)\nclf.fit(X)\nm['anomaly']=-clf.score_samples(X)\nprint(m.sort_values('anomaly',ascending=False)[['employee_id','role','seniority_level','anomaly']+feats].head(25).to_string(index=False))\nPY\"","aggregated_output":"","exit_code":null,"status":"in_progress"}}
